 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)
let snake_to_camel =
  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with
    | None -> s
    | Some (i, _) ->

 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)
let snake_to_camel =
  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with
    | None -> s
    | Some (i, _) ->

 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)
let snake_to_camel =
  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with

 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)
let snake_to_camel =
  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with
    | None -> s
    | Some (i, _) ->
        let s' = String.sub s 0 i in
        let s'' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i) in
        let s''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 1) in

  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with
    | None -> s
    | Some (i, _) ->
        let s' = String.sub s 0 i in
        let s'' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i) in
        let s''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 1) in
        let s'''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 2) in
        let s''''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 3) in

        let s''''''''''''''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 10) in

 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)

 (* Write a function to convert a snake case string to camel case string. *)
let snake_to_camel =
  let rec snake_to_camel s =
    match String.find_char s ' ' with
    | None -> s
    | Some (i, _) ->
        let s' = String.sub s 0 i in
        let s'' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i) in
        let s''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 1) in
        let s'''' = String.sub s i (String.length s - i - 2) in
